<s> footnote 5 francis wilks esq a director in the south sea company died july 5 <\s>
<s> _gentleman s magazine xii <\s>
<s> he had been agent in london for the massachusetts house of representatives since 1728 and for connecticut since 1730 <\s>
<s> 353 describes him as a merchant in london who ... <\s>
<s> was universally esteemed for his great probity as well as his humane obliging disposition footnote 6 impressment of seamen footnote 7 zachariah bourryau merchant of southampton row london and blighborough manor lincolnshire <\s>
<s> he was of a french family settled in st <\s>
<s> he died in 1752 leaving an estate of about Â £ 40,000 <\s>
<s> decree of vice-admiralty judge <\s>
<s> july 7 1742 1 footnote 1 massachusetts historical society colony of rhode island etc <\s>
<s> curia admiralitatis james allen etc <\s>
<s> proponents against the schooner _st <\s>
<s> joseph _de las animas for gunns ammunition one slave and cargo etc <\s>
<s> having maturely considered the evidence in this case as well as the examination of francisco perdomo capt <\s>
<s> of the spanish privateer who being duly notified of the trial and here in court and being asked what he had to offer why sentence of condemnation should not be passed against the said schooner her gunns ammunition rigging tackle apparel and furniture etc <\s>
<s> to which he answered he had taken several prizes and had had them condemned and his vessel etc according to the laws of nations and rules of war was a good prize and therefore he had nothing to gainsay the condemnation <\s>
<s> i therefore adjudge and decree the said schooner and her gunns cables anchors rigging sails tackle apparel with the slave and her cargo etc <\s>
<s> mentioned in the libel to be condemned as good and lawful prize to and for the use of the captors and owners of the said sloop _revenge_ to be divided according to the articles made between them <\s>
<s> i further decree the owners of the _revenge_ and the captors to pay the lawful charge of condemnation and all incident charges <\s>
<s> judge 2 newport july 7th 1742 <\s>
<s> the above is a true copy taken from the original and compared by me <\s>

<s> any of your favours <\s>
<s> this serves to inclose you dr <\s>
<s> andrews opinion 2 relating to your capture of smiths brigt <\s>
<s> which as it is of your side and agreable to that of dr <\s>
<s> paul we shall proceed in the appeal and hope for success but as their lordships in councill 3 will not sitt to hear appeals till february next you will have time en'o to give us your farther directions about it and you may depend on our serving your interest as if our own <\s>
<s> there is lately an order come to the navy office for making out bills for the hire of american transports which the commrs <\s>
<s> have promised to comply with so hope this will soon be ended and we shall hearafter acquaint you with our farther proceedings <\s>

<s> 153 footnote 3 the commission to hear appeals generally included at this time the whole privy council london 13 augt 1742 <\s>
<s> _sir confirming the foregoing copy of our last are not favd <\s>
<s> with any of yours <\s>
<s> this serves to inclose you copy of yr case abt <\s>
<s> _sarah_ and the opinion of the 3 doctors of the civill law <\s>
<s> was not i conceive extinguished by its being taken again by the spanish merchant ship she not being carried _intra praesidia 5 but only plundered and let go <\s>
<s> the pretence of a gift thereof to captn <\s>
<s> smith can have no weight for the spanish mercht <\s>
<s> acquir'd no property by the capture and could transfer none to smith who has deliver'd the cargo to the owners and freighters to which he would have had as much right as to the ship <\s>
<s> as the pretended gift could transfer no property it could extinguish no right which had been acquir'd by the _revenge_ except as to such part of the cargo as was taken away by the spaniard <\s>
<s> but the owners and company of the _revenge_ are intitled to a moiety of the full value of the ship and cargo as she arriv'd at boston without any deduction and i am of opinion that there is just ground of appeal from the sentence given in the court of admiralty there <\s>
<s> footnote 5 within the places of safety such as ports or fleets <\s>
<s> movable goods carried _intra praesidia of the enemy become clearly and fully his property and consequently if retaken vest entirely in the recaptors <\s>
<s> the same is to be said of ships carried into the enemy's ports and afterwards recaptured <\s>
<s> bynkershoek _quaestiones juris publici lib <\s>

<s> we are very sorry to have occasion to inform you that our good friend and partner francis wilks esqr departed this life the 5th instant 5 he had been in a very ill state of health for above two years past and the whole business of the house has been transacted by us for that time and we hope to the satisfaction of all our friends who we flatter our selves will continue their favors to us and we shall be ready to serve you and promote yr <\s>
<s> interest to the best of our capacity and assure you with great fidelity <\s>

<s> decree of vice-admiralty judge <\s>
<s> july 7 1742 1 footnote 1 massachusetts historical society colony of rhode island etc <\s>
<s> curia admiralitatis james allen etc <\s>
<s> proponents against the schooner _st <\s>
<s> joseph _de las animas for gunns ammunition one slave and cargo etc <\s>
<s> having maturely considered the evidence in this case as well as the examination of francisco perdomo capt <\s>
<s> of the spanish privateer who being duly notified of the trial and here in court and being asked what he had to offer why sentence of condemnation should not be passed against the said schooner her gunns ammunition rigging tackle apparel and furniture etc <\s>
<s> to which he answered he had taken several prizes and had had them condemned and his vessel etc according to the laws of nations and rules of war was a good prize and therefore he had nothing to gainsay the condemnation <\s>
<s> i therefore adjudge and decree the said schooner and her gunns cables anchors rigging sails tackle apparel with the slave and her cargo etc <\s>
<s> mentioned in the libel to be condemned as good and lawful prize to and for the use of the captors and owners of the said sloop _revenge_ to be divided according to the articles made between them <\s>
<s> i further decree the owners of the _revenge_ and the captors to pay the lawful charge of condemnation and all incident charges <\s>
<s> judge 2 newport july 7th 1742 <\s>
<s> the above is a true copy taken from the original and compared by me <\s>
